\"Firefox's CSS calc() expression handling spans both Rust (servo/style) and C++ (layout/style) layers.\\n\\n**CSS calc() Parsing (Rust):**\\n- `servo/components/style/values/specified/calc.rs`: The primary parser for CSS calc() and related math functions (min(), max(), clamp(), etc.). Defines `MathFunction` enum and `CalcNode` which represents a parsed calc expression tree. The `into_length_or_percentage()` method converts a parsed calc node into a `CalcLengthPercentage` value with an associated `clamping_mode`.\\n- `servo/components/style/values/generics/calc.rs`: Generic calc node tree structures and the `resolve_internal()` function that evaluates a calc expression tree by recursively resolving Sum, Product, MinMax, Clamp, Round, and other nodes.\\n\\n**Numeric Overflow Handling During Calc() Value Resolution:**\\n\\n1. **Rust layer** (`servo/components/style/values/computed/length_percentage.rs`): The `CalcLengthPercentage::resolve()` function resolves a computed calc length-percentage by calling `resolve_map` to substitute percentage leaves and then applies `self.clamping_mode.clamp(px.px())` to clamp the result.\\n\\n2. **Rust clamping** (`servo/components/style_traits/values.rs`): `AllowedNumericType::clamp()` enforces numeric range constraints (All, NonNegative, AtLeastOne, ZeroToOne) to prevent out-of-range values.\\n\\n3. **FFI bridge** (`servo/ports/geckolib/glue.rs`): `Servo_ResolveCalcLengthPercentage()` is the C-callable FFI function that bridges C++ layout code to Rust's calc resolution.\\n\\n4. **C++ layer** (`layout/style/ServoStyleConstsInlines.h`): Contains the key overflow-clamping code for converting resolved CSS pixel values to layout coordinates (nscoord):\\n   - `detail::DefaultLengthToAppUnits()`: Explicitly checks for values >= nscoord_MAX or <= nscoord_MIN and clamps them, preventing integer overflow when CSS calc() produces extreme values.\\n   - `detail::DefaultPercentLengthToAppUnits()`: Uses `NSToCoordTruncClamped()` which also clamps to nscoord limits.\\n   - `StyleCalcLengthPercentage::Resolve()`: Resolves a calc value to an nscoord using the provided rounder (which does the clamping).\\n   - `LengthPercentage::Resolve()`: The main resolution entry point that dispatches to the appropriate path for length, percentage, or calc values.\\n\\nThe crash with extreme values would occur in the C++ `DefaultLengthToAppUnits` path if the nscoord overflow clamping was absent or incorrect, or in the Rust `resolve_internal` path if arithmetic operations on extreme f32 values produced overflow (though f32 arithmetic in Rust doesn't panic on overflow - it produces infinity or NaN, which are then handled by the clamping logic).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1688,"cache_read_input_tokens":57547,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1688,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"db476c85-0c45-49fe-b42b-9180f3245607","uuid":"ede51d51-a2fd-4f6b-ba5b-d3ebba72f28e"}
